	internal virtual Panel PaneEchoA
	{
		get
		{
			return _PaneEchoA;
		}
		[MethodImpl(MethodImplOptions.Synchronized)]
		set
		{
			EventHandler eventHandler = PaneEchoA_Click;
			if (_PaneEchoA != null)
			{
				((Control)_PaneEchoA).DoubleClick -= eventHandler;
			}
			_PaneEchoA = value;
			if (_PaneEchoA != null)
			{
				((Control)_PaneEchoA).DoubleClick += eventHandler;
			}
		}
	}

	[DebuggerNonUserCode]
	protected override void Dispose(bool disposing)
	{
		try
		{
			if (disposing && components != null)
			{
				components.Dispose();
			}
		}
		finally
		{
			((Form)this).Dispose(disposing);
		}
	}
